tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">MongoDB - Operações CREATE (INSERT)</h1><a id="user-content-mongodb---operações-create-insert" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: MongoDB - <div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">📝 Introdução</h2><a id="user-content--introdução" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 📝 Introdução" href="#-introdução"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">As operações <strong>CREATE</strong> no MongoDB são realizadas através dos comandos <code>insertOne()</code> e <code>insertMany()</code>. Estes comandos permitem inserir novos documentos (registros) em uma coleção (equivalente a uma tabela em SQL).</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🎯 Comandos Básicos</h2><a id="user-content--comandos-básicos" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🎯 Comandos Básicos" href="#-comandos-básicos"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><code>insertOne()</code> - Inserir um único documento</h3><a id="user-content-insertone---inserir-um-único-documento" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: insertOne() - Inserir um único documento" href="#insertone---inserir-um-único-documento"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Insere um único documento em uma coleção.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Sintaxe:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="db.colecao.insertOne({
  campo1: valor1,
  campo2: valor2,
  ...
})"><pre><span class="pl-s1">db</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">colecao</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">insertOne</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">campo1</span>: <span class="pl-s1">valor1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">campo2</span>: <span class="pl-s1">valor2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  ...
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Exemplo:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="db.pacientes.insertOne({
  &quot;nome&quot;: &quot;João Silva&quot;,
  &quot;data_nascimento&quot;: ISODate(&quot;1990-05-15&quot;),
  &quot;altura&quot;: 1.80,
  &quot;documentos&quot;: {
    &quot;CPF&quot;: &quot;12345678900&quot;,
    &quot;RG&quot;: &quot;MG1234567&quot;
  }
})"><pre><span class="pl-s1">db</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">pacientes</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">insertOne</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"nome"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"João Silva"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"data_nascimento"</span>: <span class="pl-v">ISODate</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"1990-05-15"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"altura"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">1.80</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"documentos"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"CPF"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"12345678900"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"RG"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"MG1234567"</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Retorno:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
  &quot;acknowledged&quot;: true,
  &quot;insertedId&quot;: ObjectId(&quot;507f1f77bcf86cd799439011&quot;)
}"><pre><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"acknowledged"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"insertedId"</span>: <span class="pl-v">ObjectId</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"507f1f77bcf86cd799439011"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><code>insertMany()</code> - Inserir múltiplos documentos</h3><a id="user-content-insertmany---inserir-múltiplos-documentos" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: insertMany() - Inserir múltiplos documentos" href="#insertmany---inserir-múltiplos-documentos"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Insere vários documentos de uma vez em uma coleção.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Sintaxe:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="db.colecao.insertMany([
  { campo1: valor1, campo2: valor2 },
  { campo1: valor3, campo2: valor4 },
  ...
])"><pre><span class="pl-s1">db</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">colecao</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">insertMany</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">campo1</span>: <span class="pl-s1">valor1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">campo2</span>: <span class="pl-s1">valor2</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">campo1</span>: <span class="pl-s1">valor3</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">campo2</span>: <span class="pl-s1">valor4</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  ...
<span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Exemplo:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="db.pacientes.insertMany([
  {
    &quot;nome&quot;: &quot;Maria Santos&quot;,
    &quot;data_nascimento&quot;: ISODate(&quot;1985-03-20&quot;),
    &quot;altura&quot;: 1.65

    &quot;data_nascimento&quot;: ISODate(&quot;1992-07-10&quot;),
    &quot;altura&quot;: 1.75
  }
])"><pre><span class="pl-s1">db</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">pacientes</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">insertMany</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"nome"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Maria Santos"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"data_nascimento"</span>: <span class="pl-v">ISODate</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"1985-03-20"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"altura"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">1.65</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"nome"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Pedro Oliveira"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"data_nascimento"</span>: <span class="pl-v">ISODate</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"1992-07-10"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"altura"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">1.75</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Retorno:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
  &quot;acknowledged&quot;: true,
  &quot;insertedIds&quot;: [
    ObjectId(&quot;507f1f77bcf86cd799439012&quot;),
    ObjectId(&quot;507f1f77bcf86cd799439013&quot;)
  ]
}"><pre><span class="pl-kos">{</span>

    <span class="pl-v">ObjectId</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"507f1f77bcf86cd799439012"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-v">ObjectId</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"507f1f77bcf86cd799439013"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">]</span>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🔑 Tipos de Dados no MongoDB</h2><a id="user-content--tipos-de-dados-no-mongodb" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🔑 Tipos de Dados no MongoDB" href="#-tipos-de-dados-no-mongodb"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Tipos Básicos</h3><a id="user-content-tipos-básicos" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Tipos Básicos" href="#tipos-básicos"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Tipo</th>
<th>Descrição</th>
<th>Exemplo</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><strong>String</strong></td>
<td>Texto</td>
<td><code>"João Silva"</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>Number</strong></td>
<td>Números (inteiros ou decimais)</td>
<td><code>1.75</code>, <code>30</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>Boolean</strong></td>
<td>Verdadeiro ou falso</td>
<td><code>true</code>, <code>false</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>Date</strong></td>
<td>Data e hora</td>
<td><code>ISODate("2024-01-15")</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>ObjectId</strong></td>
<td>Identificador único do MongoDB</td>
<td><code>ObjectId("507f1...")</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>Array</strong></td>
<td>Lista de valores</td>
<td><code>["Cardiologia", "Clínica Geral"]</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>Object</strong></td>
<td>Documento aninhado</td>
<td><code>{cidade: "SP", estado: "SP"}</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><strong>Null</strong></td>
<td>Valor nulo/ausente</td>
<td><code>null</code></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Exemplos de Tipos</h3><a id="user-content-exemplos-de-tipos" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Exemplos de Tipos" href="#exemplos-de-tipos"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="db.exemplo.insertOne({

  <span class="pl-c">// Array</span>

  <span class="pl-c">// Object (subdocumento)</span>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🏗️ Estruturas de Dados</h2><a id="user-content-️-estruturas-de-dados" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🏗️ Estruturas de Dados" href="#️-estruturas-de-dados"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Documentos Simples</h3><a id="user-content-documentos-simples" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Documentos Simples" href="#documentos-simples"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Documentos com Subdocumentos (Objetos Aninhados)</h3><a id="user-content-documentos-com-subdocumentos-objetos-aninhados" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Documentos com Subdocumentos (Objetos Aninhados)" href="#documentos-com-subdocumentos-objetos-aninhados"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="db.pacientes.insertOne({
  &quot;nome&quot;: &quot;Ana Costa&quot;,
  &quot;endereco&quot;: {
    &quot;logradouro&quot;: &quot;Rua das Flores&quot;,
    &quot;numero&quot;: &quot;100&quot;,
    &quot;bairro&quot;: &quot;Centro&quot;,
    &quot;cidade&quot;: &quot;São Paulo&quot;,
    &quot;estado&quot;: &quot;SP&quot;,
    &quot;CEP&quot;: &quot;01000000&quot;
  },
  &quot;contato&quot;: {
    &quot;telefone&quot;: &quot;11999999999&quot;,
    &quot;email&quot;: &quot;ana@email.com&quot;
  }
})"><pre><span class="pl-s1">db</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">pacientes</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">insertOne</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"nome"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Ana Costa"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"endereco"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"logradouro"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Rua das Flores"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"numero"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"100"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"bairro"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Centro"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"cidade"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"São Paulo"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"estado"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"SP"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"CEP"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"01000000"</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"contato"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"telefone"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"11999999999"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"email"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"ana@email.com"</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Vantagem:</strong> Agrupa informações relacionadas em um único documento, facilitando consultas.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Documentos com Arrays</h3><a id="user-content-documentos-com-arrays" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Documentos com Arrays" href="#documentos-com-arrays"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="db.medicos.insertOne({
  &quot;nome&quot;: &quot;Dra. Beatriz Santos&quot;,
  &quot;especialidades&quot;: [
    &quot;Pediatria&quot;,
    &quot;Infectologia&quot;,
    &quot;Clínica Geral&quot;
  ],
  &quot;telefones&quot;: [
    &quot;11988888888&quot;,
    &quot;11977777777&quot;
  ]
})"><pre><span class="pl-s1">db</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">medicos</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">insertOne</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"nome"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Dra. Beatriz Santos"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"especialidades"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"Pediatria"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"Infectologia"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"Clínica Geral"</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"telefones"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"11988888888"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"11977777777"</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">]</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Vantagem:</strong> Permite armazenar múltiplos valores do mesmo tipo sem criar coleções separadas.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Arrays de Objetos</h3><a id="user-content-arrays-de-objetos" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Arrays de Objetos" href="#arrays-de-objetos"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="db.consultas.insertOne({

  <span class="pl-s">"paciente_id"</span>: <span class="pl-v">ObjectId</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"507f1f77bcf86cd799439011"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"data"</span>: <span class="pl-v">ISODate</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"2024-01-15"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>

      <span class="pl-s">"frequencia"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"12 em 12 horas"</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">]</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🎨 Boas Práticas</h2><a id="user-content--boas-práticas" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🎨 Boas Práticas" href="#-boas-práticas"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">1. Use <code>_id</code> Customizado (Opcional)</h3><a id="user-content-1-use-_id-customizado-opcional" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 1. Use _id Customizado (Opcional)" href="#1-use-_id-customizado-opcional"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Por padrão, o MongoDB cria um <code>_id</code> automaticamente. Mas você pode definir seu próprio:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="db.pacientes.insertOne({
  &quot;_id&quot;: &quot;PAC001&quot;,  // ID customizado
  &quot;nome&quot;: &quot;José Santos&quot;,
  &quot;CPF&quot;: &quot;12345678900&quot;
})"><pre><span class="pl-s1">db</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">pacientes</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">insertOne</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"_id"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"PAC001"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>  <span class="pl-c">// ID customizado</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"nome"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"José Santos"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"CPF"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"12345678900"</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="warning">⚠️</g-emoji> Atenção:</strong> Se você definir um <code>_id</code> que já existe, a operação falhará.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">2. Valide Dados Antes de Inserir</h3><a id="user-content-2-valide-dados-antes-de-inserir" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 2. Valide Dados Antes de Inserir" href="#2-valide-dados-antes-de-inserir"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// ❌ Evite inserir dados incompletos
db.pacientes.insertOne({
  &quot;nome&quot;: &quot;Maria&quot;
  // Faltam campos importantes
})

// ✅ Prefira inserir documentos completos
db.pacientes.insertOne({
  &quot;nome&quot;: &quot;Maria Silva&quot;,
  &quot;data_nascimento&quot;: ISODate(&quot;1990-05-20&quot;),
  &quot;CPF&quot;: &quot;12345678900&quot;,
  &quot;telefone&quot;: &quot;11999999999&quot;
})"><pre><span class="pl-c">// ❌ Evite inserir dados incompletos</span>
<span class="pl-s1">db</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">pacientes</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">insertOne</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"nome"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Maria"</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// Faltam campos importantes</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>

<span class="pl-c">// ✅ Prefira inserir documentos completos</span>
<span class="pl-s1">db</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">pacientes</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">insertOne</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"nome"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Maria Silva"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"data_nascimento"</span>: <span class="pl-v">ISODate</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"1990-05-20"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"CPF"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"12345678900"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"telefone"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"11999999999"</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">3. Mantenha Estrutura Consistente</h3><a id="user-content-3-mantenha-estrutura-consistente" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 3. Mantenha Estrutura Consistente" href="#3-mantenha-estrutura-consistente"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// ✅ Boa prática - estrutura consistente
db.pacientes.insertMany([
  {
    nome: &quot;João&quot;,
    idade: 30,
    endereco: { cidade: &quot;SP&quot;, estado: &quot;SP&quot; }
  },
  {
    nome: &quot;Maria&quot;,
    idade: 25,
    endereco: { cidade: &quot;RJ&quot;, estado: &quot;RJ&quot; }
  }
])

// ❌ Evite estruturas inconsistentes
db.pacientes.insertMany([
  {
    nome: &quot;João&quot;,
    idade: 30,
    endereco: { cidade: &quot;SP&quot; }
  },
  {
    nome: &quot;Maria&quot;,
    anos: 25,  // Campo diferente
    end: &quot;Rua X&quot;  // Estrutura diferente
  }
])"><pre><span class="pl-c">// ✅ Boa prática - estrutura consistente</span>
<span class="pl-s1">db</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">pacientes</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">insertMany</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">nome</span>: <span class="pl-s">"João"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">idade</span>: <span class="pl-c1">30</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">endereco</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">cidade</span>: <span class="pl-s">"SP"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">estado</span>: <span class="pl-s">"SP"</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">nome</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Maria"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">idade</span>: <span class="pl-c1">25</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">endereco</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">cidade</span>: <span class="pl-s">"RJ"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">estado</span>: <span class="pl-s">"RJ"</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>

<span class="pl-c">// ❌ Evite estruturas inconsistentes</span>
<span class="pl-s1">db</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">pacientes</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">insertMany</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">nome</span>: <span class="pl-s">"João"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">idade</span>: <span class="pl-c1">30</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">endereco</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">cidade</span>: <span class="pl-s">"SP"</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">nome</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Maria"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">anos</span>: <span class="pl-c1">25</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>  <span class="pl-c">// Campo diferente</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">end</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Rua X"</span>  <span class="pl-c">// Estrutura diferente</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">4. Use ISODate para Datas</h3><a id="user-content-4-use-isodate-para-datas" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 4. Use ISODate para Datas" href="#4-use-isodate-para-datas"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// ✅ Correto - use ISODate()
db.consultas.insertOne({
  data: ISODate(&quot;2024-01-15T10:30:00Z&quot;)
})

// ❌ Evite strings para datas
db.consultas.insertOne({
  data: &quot;15/01/2024&quot;  // Não permite comparações eficientes
})"><pre><span class="pl-c">// ✅ Correto - use ISODate()</span>
<span class="pl-s1">db</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">consultas</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">insertOne</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">data</span>: <span class="pl-v">ISODate</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"2024-01-15T10:30:00Z"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>

<span class="pl-c">// ❌ Evite strings para datas</span>
<span class="pl-s1">db</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">consultas</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">insertOne</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">data</span>: <span class="pl-s">"15/01/2024"</span>  <span class="pl-c">// Não permite comparações eficientes</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🔗 Relacionamentos entre Coleções</h2><a id="user-content--relacionamentos-entre-coleções" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🔗 Relacionamentos entre Coleções" href="#-relacionamentos-entre-coleções"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Abordagem 1: Referência (Reference)</h3><a id="user-content-abordagem-1-referência-reference" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Abordagem 1: Referência (Reference)" href="#abordagem-1-referência-reference"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Similar a chaves estrangeiras em SQL:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// Inserir médico
db.medicos.insertOne({
  &quot;_id&quot;: ObjectId(&quot;507f1f77bcf86cd799439011&quot;),
  &quot;nome&quot;: &quot;Dr. Carlos Silva&quot;
})

// Inserir consulta que referencia o médico
db.consultas.insertOne({
  &quot;data&quot;: ISODate(&quot;2024-01-15&quot;),
  &quot;medico_id&quot;: ObjectId(&quot;507f1f77bcf86cd799439011&quot;),  // Referência
  &quot;paciente_id&quot;: ObjectId(&quot;507f1f77bcf86cd799439012&quot;)
})"><pre><span class="pl-c">// Inserir médico</span>
<span class="pl-s1">db</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">medicos</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">insertOne</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"_id"</span>: <span class="pl-v">ObjectId</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"507f1f77bcf86cd799439011"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"nome"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Dr. Carlos Silva"</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Inserir consulta que referencia o médico</span>
<span class="pl-s1">db</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">consultas</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">insertOne</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"data"</span>: <span class="pl-v">ISODate</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"2024-01-15"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"medico_id"</span>: <span class="pl-v">ObjectId</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"507f1f77bcf86cd799439011"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>  <span class="pl-c">// Referência</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"paciente_id"</span>: <span class="pl-v">ObjectId</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"507f1f77bcf86cd799439012"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Vantagens:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Evita duplicação de dados</li>
<li>Facilita atualizações (mudar nome do médico em um só lugar)</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Desvantagens:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Requer múltiplas consultas ou uso de <code>$lookup</code> (JOIN)</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Abordagem 2: Embedding (Documentos Aninhados)</h3><a id="user-content-abordagem-2-embedding-documentos-aninhados" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Abordagem 2: Embedding (Documentos Aninhados)" href="#abordagem-2-embedding-documentos-aninhados"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Incorporar documentos relacionados:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="db.consultas.insertOne({
  &quot;data&quot;: ISODate(&quot;2024-01-15&quot;),
  &quot;medico&quot;: {
    &quot;nome&quot;: &quot;Dr. Carlos Silva&quot;,
    &quot;CRM&quot;: &quot;SP123456&quot;,
    &quot;especialidade&quot;: &quot;Cardiologia&quot;
  },
  &quot;paciente&quot;: {
    &quot;nome&quot;: &quot;João Santos&quot;,
    &quot;CPF&quot;: &quot;12345678900&quot;
  }
})"><pre><span class="pl-s1">db</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">consultas</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">insertOne</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"data"</span>: <span class="pl-v">ISODate</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"2024-01-15"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"medico"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"nome"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Dr. Carlos Silva"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"CRM"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"SP123456"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"especialidade"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Cardiologia"</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s">"paciente"</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"nome"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"João Santos"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"CPF"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"12345678900"</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Vantagens:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Uma única consulta retorna todos os dados</li>
<li>Melhor performance para leitura</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Desvantagens:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Duplicação de dados</li>
<li>Se o médico mudar de nome, precisa atualizar em vários lugares</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">💡 Comparação com SQL</h2><a id="user-content--comparação-com-sql" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 💡 Comparação com SQL" href="#-comparação-com-sql"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>SQL</th>
<th>MongoDB</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>INSERT INTO pacientes (nome, idade) VALUES ('João', 30)</code></td>
<td><code>db.pacientes.insertOne({nome: "João", idade: 30})</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>INSERT INTO pacientes ... ; INSERT INTO ...</code></td>
<td><code>db.pacientes.insertMany([{...}, {...}])</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Tabela</td>
<td>Coleção</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Linha/Registro</td>
<td>Documento</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Coluna</td>
<td>Campo</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Chave Primária</td>
<td><code>_id</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Chave Estrangeira</td>
<td>Referência (ObjectId) ou Embedding</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🚀 Comandos Úteis</h2><a id="user-content--comandos-úteis" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🚀 Comandos Úteis" href="#-comandos-úteis"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Verificar se a inserção foi bem-sucedida</h3><a id="user-content-verificar-se-a-inserção-foi-bem-sucedida" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Verificar se a inserção foi bem-sucedida" href="#verificar-se-a-inserção-foi-bem-sucedida"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="const resultado = db.pacientes.insertOne({nome: &quot;João&quot;})
console.log(resultado.acknowledged)  // true se sucesso
console.log(resultado.insertedId)     // ObjectId do documento inserido"><pre><span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">resultado</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">db</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">pacientes</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">insertOne</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">nome</span>: <span class="pl-s">"João"</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
<span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">resultado</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">acknowledged</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>  <span class="pl-c">// true se sucesso</span>
<span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">resultado</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">insertedId</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>     <span class="pl-c">// ObjectId do documento inserido</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Inserir com tratamento de erro</h3><a id="user-content-inserir-com-tratamento-de-erro" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Inserir com tratamento de erro" href="#inserir-com-tratamento-de-erro"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="try {
  db.pacientes.insertOne({
    &quot;_id&quot;: &quot;PAC001&quot;,
    &quot;nome&quot;: &quot;Maria Silva&quot;
  })
} catch (error) {
  console.log(&quot;Erro ao inserir:&quot;, error.message)
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">try</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">db</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">pacientes</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">insertOne</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"_id"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"PAC001"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"nome"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Maria Silva"</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">catch</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"Erro ao inserir:"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">message</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Inserir múltiplos documentos com opção ordered</h3><a id="user-content-inserir-múltiplos-documentos-com-opção-ordered" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Inserir múltiplos documentos com opção ordered" href="#inserir-múltiplos-documentos-com-opção-ordered"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// ordered: true (padrão) - para no primeiro erro
db.pacientes.insertMany([
  {nome: &quot;João&quot;},
  {_id: 1, nome: &quot;Maria&quot;},
  {_id: 1, nome: &quot;Pedro&quot;}  // Vai falhar (ID duplicado)
  // Os documentos seguintes NÃO serão inseridos
], {ordered: true})

// ordered: false - continua mesmo com erros
db.pacientes.insertMany([
  {nome: &quot;João&quot;},
  {_id: 1, nome: &quot;Maria&quot;},
  {_id: 1, nome: &quot;Pedro&quot;},  // Vai falhar
  {nome: &quot;Ana&quot;}  // Mas este será inserido
], {ordered: false})"><pre><span class="pl-c">// ordered: true (padrão) - para no primeiro erro</span>
<span class="pl-s1">db</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">pacientes</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">insertMany</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">nome</span>: <span class="pl-s">"João"</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">_id</span>: <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">nome</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Maria"</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">_id</span>: <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">nome</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Pedro"</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>  <span class="pl-c">// Vai falhar (ID duplicado)</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// Os documentos seguintes NÃO serão inseridos</span>
<span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">ordered</span>: <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>

<span class="pl-c">// ordered: false - continua mesmo com erros</span>
<span class="pl-s1">db</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">pacientes</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">insertMany</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">nome</span>: <span class="pl-s">"João"</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">_id</span>: <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">nome</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Maria"</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">_id</span>: <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">nome</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Pedro"</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>  <span class="pl-c">// Vai falhar</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">nome</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Ana"</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>  <span class="pl-c">// Mas este será inserido</span>
<span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">ordered</span>: <span class="pl-c1">false</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">📚 Operadores Especiais em Inserção</h2><a id="user-content--operadores-especiais-em-inserção" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 📚 Operadores Especiais em Inserção" href="#-operadores-especiais-em-inserção"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><code>$currentDate</code> - Data/hora atual</h3><a id="user-content-currentdate---datahora-atual" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: $currentDate - Data/hora atual" href="#currentdate---datahora-atual"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="db.logs.insertOne({
  evento: &quot;Login&quot;,
  usuario: &quot;joao&quot;,
  timestamp: new Date()  // Data/hora atual
})"><pre><span class="pl-s1">db</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">logs</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">insertOne</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">evento</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Login"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">usuario</span>: <span class="pl-s">"joao"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">timestamp</span>: <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">Date</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>  <span class="pl-c">// Data/hora atual</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><code>$inc</code> - Não aplicável diretamente em INSERT</h3><a id="user-content-inc---não-aplicável-diretamente-em-insert" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: $inc - Não aplicável diretamente em INSERT" href="#inc---não-aplicável-diretamente-em-insert"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Operadores como <code>$inc</code>, <code>$set</code>, <code>$push</code> são usados em UPDATE, não em INSERT.</p>
<hr>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Exercício 3: Inserir Documento com Subdocumentos</h3><a id="user-content-exercício-3-inserir-documento-com-subdocumentos" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Exercício 3: Inserir Documento com Subdocumentos" href="#exercício-3-inserir-documento-com-subdocumentos"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🔍 Verificando Suas Inserções</h2><a id="user-content--verificando-suas-inserções" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🔍 Verificando Suas Inserções" href="#-verificando-suas-inserções"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Após inserir documentos, você pode verificá-los com:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// Ver todos os documentos
db.pacientes.find()

// Ver de forma formatada
db.pacientes.find().pretty()

// Contar documentos
db.pacientes.countDocuments()

// Ver o último documento inserido
db.pacientes.find().sort({_id: -1}).limit(1)"><pre><span class="pl-c">// Ver todos os documentos</span>
<span class="pl-s1">db</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">pacientes</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">find</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Ver de forma formatada</span>
<span class="pl-s1">db</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">pacientes</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">find</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">pretty</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Contar documentos</span>
<span class="pl-s1">db</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">pacientes</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">countDocuments</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Ver o último documento inserido</span>
<span class="pl-s1">db</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">pacientes</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">find</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">sort</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">_id</span>: <span class="pl-c1">-</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">limit</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span></pre></div>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">📖 Recursos Adicionais</h2><a id="user-content--recursos-adicionais" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 📖 Recursos Adicionais" href="#-recursos-adicionais"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Documentação Oficial:</strong> <a href="https://docs.mongodb.com/manual/reference/method/db.collection.insertOne/" rel="nofollow">MongoDB Insert</a></li>
<li><strong>Schema Design:</strong> Como estruturar seus documentos</li>
<li><strong>Validação de Schema:</strong> Como garantir que documentos sigam regras específicas</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🎓 Resumo</h2><a id="user-content--resumo" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🎓 Resumo" href="#-resumo"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong><code>insertOne()</code></strong>: Insere um documento</li>
<li><strong><code>insertMany()</code></strong>: Insere múltiplos documentos</li>
<li><strong>Documentos</strong>: Estruturas flexíveis (não precisam seguir um schema rígido)</li>
<li><strong>Subdocumentos</strong>: Objetos aninhados para agrupar dados relacionados</li>
<li><strong>Arrays</strong>: Listas de valores ou objetos</li>
<li><strong><code>_id</code></strong>: Identificador único (criado automaticamente ou customizado)</li>
<li><strong>Referências vs Embedding</strong>: Duas formas de relacionar dados</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Agora você está pronto para criar documentos no MongoDB! 🚀</p>
